           <p>
            So I'd like to change the
            <code>
             android:fontFamily
            </code>
            in Android but I don't see any pre-defined fonts in Android. How do I select one of the pre-defined ones? I don't really need to define my own TypeFace but all I need is something different from what it shows right now.
           </p>
           <pre><code>&lt;TextView
    android:id="@+id/HeaderText"
    android:layout_width="wrap_content"
    android:layout_height="wrap_content"
    android:layout_alignParentTop="true"
    android:layout_centerHorizontal="true"
    android:layout_marginTop="52dp"
    android:gravity="center"
    android:text="CallerBlocker"
    android:textSize="40dp"
    android:fontFamily="Arial"
 /&gt;
</code></pre>
           <p>
            It seems what I did up there won't really work! BTW
            <code>
             android:fontFamily="Arial"
            </code>
            was a stupid attempt!
           </p>

           </div>
          </div>

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer accepted-answer" data-answerid="13329907" data-highest-scored="1" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="1" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1727" id="answer-13329907" itemprop="acceptedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="13329907">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1727" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1727
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/13329907/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             From android 4.1 / 4.2 / 5.0, the following
             <a href="https://material.google.com/resources/roboto-noto-fonts.html" rel="noreferrer">
              Roboto
             </a>
             font families are available:
            </p>
            <pre><code>android:fontFamily="sans-serif"           // roboto regular
android:fontFamily="sans-serif-light"     // roboto light
android:fontFamily="sans-serif-condensed" // roboto condensed
android:fontFamily="sans-serif-black"     // roboto black
android:fontFamily="sans-serif-thin"      // roboto thin (android 4.2)
android:fontFamily="sans-serif-medium"    // roboto medium (android 5.0)
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/M2yxI.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/M2yxI.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             in combination with
            </p>
            <pre><code>android:textStyle="normal|bold|italic"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             this 16 variants are possible:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              Roboto regular
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto bold
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto bold italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Light
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Light italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Thin
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Thin italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Condensed
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Condensed italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Condensed bold
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Condensed bold italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Black
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Black italic
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Medium
             </li>
             <li>
              Roboto-Medium italic
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             <code>
              fonts.xml
             </code>
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;resources&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_light"&gt;sans-serif-light&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_medium"&gt;sans-serif-medium&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_regular"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_condensed"&gt;sans-serif-condensed&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_black"&gt;sans-serif-black&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_thin"&gt;sans-serif-thin&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;/resources&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="42976600" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="2" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="251" id="answer-42976600" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="42976600">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="251" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             251
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/42976600/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

             </svg>
            </a>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Starting from
             <strong>
              Android-Studio 3.0
             </strong>
             its very easy to change font family
            </p>
            <p>
             Using support library 26, it will work on devices running Android API version 16 and higher
            </p>
            <p>
             Create a folder
             <code>
              font
             </code>
             under
             <code>
              res
             </code>
             directory .Download the font which ever you want and paste it inside
             <code>
              font
             </code>
             folder. The structure should be some thing like below
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eiChI.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/eiChI.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Note:
             </strong>
             As of Android Support Library 26.0, you must declare both sets of attributes ( android:  and app: ) to ensure your fonts load on devices running 
 Api  26 or lower.
            </p>
            <p>
             Now you can change font in
             <strong>
              layout
             </strong>
             using
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;TextView
android:layout_width="wrap_content"
android:layout_height="wrap_content"
android:fontFamily="@font/dancing_script"
app:fontFamily="@font/dancing_script"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To change
             <strong>
              Programatically
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code> Typeface typeface = getResources().getFont(R.font.myfont);
   //or to support all versions use
Typeface typeface = ResourcesCompat.getFont(context, R.font.myfont);
 textView.setTypeface(typeface);  
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To change font using
             <strong>
              styles.xml
             </strong>
             create a style
            </p>
            <pre><code> &lt;style name="Regular"&gt;
        &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;@font/dancing_script&lt;/item&gt;
        &lt;item name="fontFamily"&gt;@font/dancing_script&lt;/item&gt;
        &lt;item name="android:textStyle"&gt;normal&lt;/item&gt;
 &lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and apply this style to
             <code>
              TextView
             </code>
            </p>
            <pre><code>  &lt;TextView
    android:layout_width="wrap_content"
    android:layout_height="wrap_content"
    style="@style/Regular"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             you can also Create your own
             <strong>
              font family
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              -
             </strong>
             Right-click the font folder and go to
             <strong>
              New &gt; Font resource file
             </strong>
             . The New Resource File window appears.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              -
             </strong>
             Enter the
             <strong>
              file name
             </strong>
             , and then click
             <strong>
              OK
             </strong>
             . The new font resource XML opens in the editor.
            </p>
            <p>
             Write your own font family here , for example
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;font-family xmlns:android="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android"&gt;
    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="normal"
        android:fontWeight="400"
        android:font="@font/lobster_regular" /&gt;
    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="italic"
        android:fontWeight="400"
        android:font="@font/lobster_italic" /&gt;
&lt;/font-family&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             this is simply a mapping of a specific fontStyle and fontWeight to the font resource which will be used to render that specific variant. Valid values for fontStyle are normal or italic; and fontWeight conforms to the
             <a href="https://www.w3.org/TR/css-fonts-3/#font-weight-numeric-values" rel="noreferrer">
              CSS font-weight specification
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              1.
             </strong>
             To
             <strong>
              change
             </strong>
             fontfamily in
             <strong>
              layout
             </strong>
             you can write
            </p>
            <pre><code> &lt;TextView
    android:layout_width="wrap_content"
    android:layout_height="wrap_content"
    android:fontFamily="@font/lobster"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             <strong>
              2.
             </strong>
             To Change
             <strong>
              Programmatically
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code> Typeface typeface = getResources().getFont(R.font.lobster);
   //or to support all versions use
Typeface typeface = ResourcesCompat.getFont(context, R.font.lobster);
 textView.setTypeface(typeface);  
</code></pre>
            <p>
             To
             <strong>
              change font of entire App
             </strong>
             Add these two lines in AppTheme
            </p>
            <pre><code> &lt;style name="AppTheme" parent="Theme.AppCompat.Light.NoActionBar"&gt;
     &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;@font/your_font&lt;/item&gt;
     &lt;item name="fontFamily"&gt;@font/your_font&lt;/item&gt;
  &lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             See the
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/ui/look-and-feel/fonts-in-xml.html" rel="noreferrer">
              Documentation
             </a>
             ,
             <a href="https://www.journaldev.com/13291/android-custom-fonts-tutorial" rel="noreferrer">
              Android Custom Fonts Tutorial
             </a>
             For more info
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

                 </code>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/6478047/manohar" title="18,959 reputation">
                  Manohar
                 </a>
                </div>
                <span class="comment-date" dir="ltr">
                 <span class="relativetime-clean" title="2018-05-03 12:30:25Z, License: CC BY-SA 4.0">
                  May 3, 2018 at 12:30
                 </span>
                </span>
               </div>
              </div>
             </li>
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="119436747" data-comment-owner-id="1324802" data-comment-score="1" id="comment-119436747">
              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">
               <div class="comment-score js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="cool" title="number of 'useful comment' votes received">

                </span>

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 Right-click main, select 'New', select 'Android Resource File'. In popup window type 'font' for name, select 'Font' from drop-down 'Resource Type' list. Click 'OK'.
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             This is the way to set the font programmatically:
            </p>
            <pre><code>TextView tv = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.appname);
Typeface face = Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(),
            "fonts/epimodem.ttf");
tv.setTypeface(face);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             put the font file in your assets folder. In my case I created a subdirectory called fonts.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              EDIT:
             </strong>
             If you wonder where is your assets folder see
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/18302603/where-to-place-assets-folder-in-android-studio">
              this question
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="29533686">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="29533686" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="4" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="108" id="answer-29533686" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="29533686">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="108" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             108
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/29533686/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I had to parse
             <code>
              /system/etc/fonts.xml
             </code>
             in a recent project. Here are the current font families as of Lollipop:
            </p>
            <pre><code>╔════╦════════════════════════════╦═════════════════════════════╗
║    ║ FONT FAMILY                ║ TTF FILE                    ║
╠════╬════════════════════════════╬═════════════════════════════╣
║  1 ║ casual                     ║ ComingSoon.ttf              ║
║  2 ║ cursive                    ║ DancingScript-Regular.ttf   ║
║  3 ║ monospace                  ║ DroidSansMono.ttf           ║
║  4 ║ sans-serif                 ║ Roboto-Regular.ttf          ║
║  5 ║ sans-serif-black           ║ Roboto-Black.ttf            ║
║  6 ║ sans-serif-condensed       ║ RobotoCondensed-Regular.ttf ║
║  7 ║ sans-serif-condensed-light ║ RobotoCondensed-Light.ttf   ║
║  8 ║ sans-serif-light           ║ Roboto-Light.ttf            ║
║  9 ║ sans-serif-medium          ║ Roboto-Medium.ttf           ║
║ 10 ║ sans-serif-smallcaps       ║ CarroisGothicSC-Regular.ttf ║
║ 11 ║ sans-serif-thin            ║ Roboto-Thin.ttf             ║
║ 12 ║ serif                      ║ NotoSerif-Regular.ttf       ║
║ 13 ║ serif-monospace            ║ CutiveMono.ttf              ║
╚════╩════════════════════════════╩═════════════════════════════╝
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             Here is the parser (based off
             <a href="https://github.com/android/platform_frameworks_base/blob/59701b9ba5c453e327bc0e6873a9f6ff87a10391/graphics/java/android/graphics/FontListParser.java">
              FontListParser
             </a>
             ):
            </p>
            <pre><code>import java.io.File;
import java.io.FileInputStream;
import java.io.IOException;
import java.io.InputStream;
import java.util.ArrayList;
import java.util.Collections;
import java.util.Comparator;
import java.util.List;

import org.xmlpull.v1.XmlPullParser;
import org.xmlpull.v1.XmlPullParserException;

import android.util.Xml;

/**
 * Helper class to get the current font families on an Android device.&lt;/p&gt;
 * 
 * Usage:&lt;/p&gt; {@code List&lt;SystemFont&gt; fonts = FontListParser.safelyGetSystemFonts();}&lt;/p&gt;
 */
public final class FontListParser {

    private static final File FONTS_XML = new File("/system/etc/fonts.xml");

    private static final File SYSTEM_FONTS_XML = new File("/system/etc/system_fonts.xml");

    public static List&lt;SystemFont&gt; getSystemFonts() throws Exception {
        String fontsXml;
        if (FONTS_XML.exists()) {
            fontsXml = FONTS_XML.getAbsolutePath();
        } else if (SYSTEM_FONTS_XML.exists()) {
            fontsXml = SYSTEM_FONTS_XML.getAbsolutePath();
        } else {
            throw new RuntimeException("fonts.xml does not exist on this system");
        }
        Config parser = parse(new FileInputStream(fontsXml));
        List&lt;SystemFont&gt; fonts = new ArrayList&lt;&gt;();

        for (Family family : parser.families) {
            if (family.name != null) {
                Font font = null;
                for (Font f : family.fonts) {
                    font = f;
                    if (f.weight == 400) {
                        break;
                    }
                }
                SystemFont systemFont = new SystemFont(family.name, font.fontName);
                if (fonts.contains(systemFont)) {
                    continue;
                }
                fonts.add(new SystemFont(family.name, font.fontName));
            }
        }

        for (Alias alias : parser.aliases) {
            if (alias.name == null || alias.toName == null || alias.weight == 0) {
                continue;
            }
            for (Family family : parser.families) {
                if (family.name == null || !family.name.equals(alias.toName)) {
                    continue;
                }
                for (Font font : family.fonts) {
                    if (font.weight == alias.weight) {
                        fonts.add(new SystemFont(alias.name, font.fontName));
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }

        if (fonts.isEmpty()) {
            throw new Exception("No system fonts found.");
        }

        Collections.sort(fonts, new Comparator&lt;SystemFont&gt;() {

            @Override
            public int compare(SystemFont font1, SystemFont font2) {
                return font1.name.compareToIgnoreCase(font2.name);
            }

        });

        return fonts;
    }

    public static List&lt;SystemFont&gt; safelyGetSystemFonts() {
        try {
            return getSystemFonts();
        } catch (Exception e) {
            String[][] defaultSystemFonts = {
                    {
                            "cursive", "DancingScript-Regular.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "monospace", "DroidSansMono.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif", "Roboto-Regular.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif-light", "Roboto-Light.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif-medium", "Roboto-Medium.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif-black", "Roboto-Black.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif-condensed", "RobotoCondensed-Regular.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "sans-serif-thin", "Roboto-Thin.ttf"
                    }, {
                            "serif", "NotoSerif-Regular.ttf"
                    }
            };
            List&lt;SystemFont&gt; fonts = new ArrayList&lt;&gt;();
            for (String[] names : defaultSystemFonts) {
                File file = new File("/system/fonts", names[1]);
                if (file.exists()) {
                    fonts.add(new SystemFont(names[0], file.getAbsolutePath()));
                }
            }
            return fonts;
        }
    }

    /* Parse fallback list (no names) */
    public static Config parse(InputStream in) throws XmlPullParserException, IOException {
        try {
            XmlPullParser parser = Xml.newPullParser();
            parser.setInput(in, null);
            parser.nextTag();
            return readFamilies(parser);
        } finally {
            in.close();
        }
    }

    private static Alias readAlias(XmlPullParser parser) throws XmlPullParserException, IOException {
        Alias alias = new Alias();
        alias.name = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "name");
        alias.toName = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "to");
        String weightStr = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "weight");
        if (weightStr == null) {
            alias.weight = 0;
        } else {
            alias.weight = Integer.parseInt(weightStr);
        }
        skip(parser); // alias tag is empty, ignore any contents and consume end tag
        return alias;
    }

    private static Config readFamilies(XmlPullParser parser) throws XmlPullParserException,
            IOException {
        Config config = new Config();
        parser.require(XmlPullParser.START_TAG, null, "familyset");
        while (parser.next() != XmlPullParser.END_TAG) {
            if (parser.getEventType() != XmlPullParser.START_TAG) {
                continue;
            }
            if (parser.getName().equals("family")) {
                config.families.add(readFamily(parser));
            } else if (parser.getName().equals("alias")) {
                config.aliases.add(readAlias(parser));
            } else {
                skip(parser);
            }
        }
        return config;
    }

    private static Family readFamily(XmlPullParser parser) throws XmlPullParserException,
            IOException {
        String name = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "name");
        String lang = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "lang");
        String variant = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "variant");
        List&lt;Font&gt; fonts = new ArrayList&lt;Font&gt;();
        while (parser.next() != XmlPullParser.END_TAG) {
            if (parser.getEventType() != XmlPullParser.START_TAG) {
                continue;
            }
            String tag = parser.getName();
            if (tag.equals("font")) {
                String weightStr = parser.getAttributeValue(null, "weight");
                int weight = weightStr == null ? 400 : Integer.parseInt(weightStr);
                boolean isItalic = "italic".equals(parser.getAttributeValue(null, "style"));
                String filename = parser.nextText();
                String fullFilename = "/system/fonts/" + filename;
                fonts.add(new Font(fullFilename, weight, isItalic));
            } else {
                skip(parser);
            }
        }
        return new Family(name, fonts, lang, variant);
    }

    private static void skip(XmlPullParser parser) throws XmlPullParserException, IOException {
        int depth = 1;
        while (depth &gt; 0) {
            switch (parser.next()) {
            case XmlPullParser.START_TAG:
                depth++;
                break;
            case XmlPullParser.END_TAG:
                depth--;
                break;
            }
        }
    }

    private FontListParser() {

    }

    public static class Alias {

        public String name;

        public String toName;

        public int weight;
    }

    public static class Config {

        public List&lt;Alias&gt; aliases;

        public List&lt;Family&gt; families;

        Config() {
            families = new ArrayList&lt;Family&gt;();
            aliases = new ArrayList&lt;Alias&gt;();
        }

    }

    public static class Family {

        public List&lt;Font&gt; fonts;

        public String lang;

        public String name;

        public String variant;

        public Family(String name, List&lt;Font&gt; fonts, String lang, String variant) {
            this.name = name;
            this.fonts = fonts;
            this.lang = lang;
            this.variant = variant;
        }

    }

    public static class Font {

        public String fontName;

        public boolean isItalic;

        public int weight;

        Font(String fontName, int weight, boolean isItalic) {
            this.fontName = fontName;
            this.weight = weight;
            this.isItalic = isItalic;
        }

    }

    public static class SystemFont {

        public String name;

        public String path;

        public SystemFont(String name, String path) {
            this.name = name;
            this.path = path;
        }

    }
}
</code></pre>
            <hr/>
            <p>
             Feel free to use the above class in your project. For example, you could give your users a selection of font families and set the typeface based on their preference.
            </p>
            <p>
             A small incomplete example:
            </p>
            <pre><code>final List&lt;FontListParser.SystemFont&gt; fonts = FontListParser.safelyGetSystemFonts();
String[] items = new String[fonts.size()];
for (int i = 0; i &lt; fonts.size(); i++) {
    items[i] = fonts.get(i).name;
}

new AlertDialog.Builder(this).setSingleChoiceItems(items, -1, new DialogInterface.OnClickListener() {
    @Override
    public void onClick(DialogInterface dialog, int which) {
        FontListParser.SystemFont selectedFont = fonts.get(which);
        // TODO: do something with the font
        Toast.makeText(getApplicationContext(), selectedFont.path, Toast.LENGTH_LONG).show();
    }
}).show();
</code></pre>
           </div>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Android doesn't allow you to set custom fonts from the XML layout. Instead, you must bundle the specific font file in your app's assets folder, and set it programmatically. Something like:
            </p>
            <pre><code>TextView textView = (TextView) findViewById(&lt;your TextView ID&gt;);
Typeface typeFace = Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(), "&lt;file name&gt;");
textView.setTypeface(typeFace);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Note that you can only run this code after setContentView() has been called. Also, only some fonts are supported by Android, and should be in a
             <code>
              .ttf (TrueType)
             </code>
             or
             <code>
              .otf (OpenType)
             </code>
             format. Even then, some fonts may not work.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="http://www.fontsquirrel.com/fonts/Chantelli-Antiqua" rel="noreferrer">
              This
             </a>
             is a font that definitely works on Android, and you can use this to confirm that your code is working in case your font file isn't supported by Android.
            </p>
            <p>
             Android O Update: This is now possible with
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html" rel="noreferrer">
              XML in Android O
             </a>
             , based on Roger's comment.
            </p>
           </div>

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 "Android doesn't allow you to set custom fonts from the XML layout." This has been changed in Android O, which allows you to create customized font family and apply them in XML:
                 <a href="https://developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
                  developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html
                 </a>
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1825443/roger-huang" title="587 reputation">
                  Roger Huang
                 </a>
                </div>

           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To set Roboto programmatically:
            </p>
            <pre><code>paint.setTypeface(Typeface.create("sans-serif-thin", Typeface.NORMAL));
</code></pre>

        <a name="26185430">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="26185430" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="7" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="30" id="answer-26185430" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="26185430">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="30" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             30
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/26185430/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you want it programatically, you could use
            </p>
            <pre><code>label.setTypeface(Typeface.SANS_SERIF, Typeface.ITALIC);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Where
             <code>
              SANS_SERIF
             </code>
             you can use:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               DEFAULT
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               DEFAULT_BOLD
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               MONOSPACE
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               SANS_SERIF
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               SERIF
              </code>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             And where
             <code>
              ITALIC
             </code>
             you can use:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              <code>
               BOLD
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               BOLD_ITALIC
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               ITALIC
              </code>
             </li>
             <li>
              <code>
               NORMAL
              </code>
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             All is stated
             <a href="http://developer.android.com/intl/es/reference/android/graphics/Typeface.html">
              on Android Developers
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="63982070" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="8" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="27" id="answer-63982070" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="63982070">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             <strong>
              Kotlin Code - Textview to set custom font from Resource Folder
             </strong>
            </p>
            <p>
             Set custom font from
             <em>
              res -&gt; font -&gt; avenir_next_regular.ttf
             </em>
            </p>
            <pre><code>textView!!.typeface = ResourcesCompat.getFont(context!!, R.font.avenir_next_regular)
</code></pre>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             It's the same as
             <code>
              android:typeface
             </code>
             .
            </p>
            <p>
             built-in fonts are:
            </p>
            <ul>
             <li>
              normal
             </li>
             <li>
              sans
             </li>
             <li>
              serif
             </li>
             <li>
              monospace
             </li>
            </ul>
            <p>
             See
             <a href="http://developer.android.com/reference/android/widget/TextView.html#attr_android:typeface" rel="noreferrer">
              android:typeface
             </a>
             .
            </p>
           </div>

              <div class="js-comment-actions comment-actions">

              <div class="comment-text js-comment-text-and-form">
               <div class="comment-body js-comment-edit-hide">
                <span class="comment-copy">
                 I don't think it is the same thing, but it does appear that we can't use both. It seems that there are now no less than three different attributes mapped to
                 <code>
                  setTypeface()
                 </code>
                 . Namely
                 <code>
                  fontFamily
                 </code>
                 ,
                 <code>
                  typeface
                 </code>
                 and
                 <code>
                  textStyle
                 </code>
                 . But I can't for the life of me figure out how these are precisely combined to resolve a concrete Typeface instance. Has anyone figured this out? Google's documentation is less than helpful...
                </span>
                <div class="d-inline-flex ai-center">
                 –
                 <a class="comment-user" href="/users/1167703/rad-haring" title="875 reputation">
                  Rad Haring
                 </a>
                </div>

        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="58299024" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="10" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="18" id="answer-58299024" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58299024">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="18" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             18
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58299024/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             One simple way is by adding the desired
             <strong>
              font
             </strong>
             in the project.
            </p>
            <p>
             Go to
             <strong>
              File-&gt;New-&gt;New Resource Directory
             </strong>
             Select
             <em>
              <strong>
               font
              </strong>
             </em>
            </p>
            <p>
             This will create a new directory,
             <strong>
              font
             </strong>
             , in your resources.
            </p>
            <p>
             Download your
             <strong>
              font (.ttf)
             </strong>
             . I use
             <a href="https://fonts.google.com" rel="noreferrer">
              https://fonts.google.com
             </a>
             for the same
            </p>
            <p>
             Add that to your
             <strong>
              fonts
             </strong>
             folder then use them in the XML or programmatically.
            </p>
            <p>
             XML -
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;TextView 
android:id="@+id/textView"
android:layout_width="wrap_content"
android:layout_height="wrap_content"
android:fontFamily="@font/your_font"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Programatically -
            </p>
            <pre><code> Typeface typeface = ResourcesCompat.getFont(this, R.font.your_font);
 textView.setTypeface(typeface); 
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

             <time datetime="2019-10-09T07:25:23" itemprop="dateCreated">

            <pre><code>Typeface typeface = ResourcesCompat.getFont(context, R.font.font_name);
textView.setTypeface(typeface);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             set easily font to any textview from res&gt;font directory programmatically
            </p>

            <p>
             I think I am too late but maybe this solution helpful for others. For using custom font place your font file in your font directory.
            </p>
            <pre><code>textView.setTypeface(ResourcesCompat.getFont(this, R.font.lato));
</code></pre>

               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/24596541/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I am using excellent library
             <a href="https://github.com/chrisjenx/Calligraphy">
              Calligraphy
             </a>
             by Chris Jenx designed to allow you to use custom fonts in your android application. Give it a try!
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             What you want is not possible. You must need to set
             <code>
              TypeFace
             </code>
             in your Code.
            </p>
            <p>
             In
             <code>
              XML
             </code>
             what you can do is
            </p>
            <pre><code>android:typeface="sans" | "serif" | "monospace"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             other then this you can not play much with the Fonts in XML. :)
            </p>
            <p>
             For
             <code>
              Arial
             </code>
             you need to set type face in your code.
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="29834998">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="29834998" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="15" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="12" id="answer-29834998" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="29834998">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="12" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             12
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/29834998/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             An easy way to manage the fonts would be to declare them via resources, as such:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;!--++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;!--added on API 16 (JB - 4.1)--&gt;
&lt;!--++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;!--the default font--&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_regular"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_light"&gt;sans-serif-light&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_condensed"&gt;sans-serif-condensed&lt;/string&gt;

&lt;!--+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;!--added on API 17 (JBMR1 - 4.2)--&gt;
&lt;!--+++++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_thin"&gt;sans-serif-thin&lt;/string&gt;

&lt;!--+++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;!--added on Lollipop (LL- 5.0)--&gt;
&lt;!--+++++++++++++++++++++++++++--&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_medium"&gt;sans-serif-medium&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_black"&gt;sans-serif-black&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;string name="fontFamily__roboto_condensed_light"&gt;sans-serif-condensed-light&lt;/string&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             This is based on the source code
             <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/base/+/lollipop-release/data/fonts/system_fonts.xml" rel="noreferrer">
              <strong>
               here
              </strong>
             </a>
             and
             <a href="https://android.googlesource.com/platform/frameworks/base/+/master/data/fonts/fonts.xml" rel="noreferrer">
              <strong>
               here
              </strong>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

                 @AZ_ Just like many resource files, you can put it in any XML file you wish, inside the "res/values/" folder . For example, put it in "res/values/fonts.xml" . And, to use it, do simply like this for example :  android:fontFamily="string/fontFamily__roboto_regular"

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="45327700">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Dynamically you can set the fontfamily similar to android:fontFamily in xml by using this,
            </p>
            <pre><code>For Custom font:

 TextView tv = ((TextView) v.findViewById(R.id.select_item_title));
 Typeface face=Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(),"fonts/mycustomfont.ttf"); 
 tv.setTypeface(face);

For Default font:

 tv.setTypeface(Typeface.create("sans-serif-medium",Typeface.NORMAL));
</code></pre>
            <p>
             These are the list of
             <strong>
              <em>
               default font
              </em>
             </strong>
             family used, use any of this by replacing the double quotation string
             <strong>
              "sans-serif-medium"
             </strong>
            </p>
            <pre><code>FONT FAMILY                    TTF FILE                    

1  casual                      ComingSoon.ttf              
2  cursive                     DancingScript-Regular.ttf   
3  monospace                   DroidSansMono.ttf           
4  sans-serif                  Roboto-Regular.ttf          
5  sans-serif-black            Roboto-Black.ttf            
6  sans-serif-condensed        RobotoCondensed-Regular.ttf 
7  sans-serif-condensed-light  RobotoCondensed-Light.ttf   
8  sans-serif-light            Roboto-Light.ttf            
9  sans-serif-medium           Roboto-Medium.ttf           
10  sans-serif-smallcaps       CarroisGothicSC-Regular.ttf 
11  sans-serif-thin            Roboto-Thin.ttf             
12  serif                      NotoSerif-Regular.ttf       
13  serif-monospace            CutiveMono.ttf              
</code></pre>
            <p>
             "mycustomfont.ttf" is the ttf file.
             <strong>
              <em>
               Path
              </em>
             </strong>
             will be in
             <em>
              src/assets/fonts/mycustomfont.ttf
             </em>
             , you can refer more about default font in this
             <a href="https://stackoverflow.com/questions/39535475/what-is-the-default-font-family-in-android#39536066">
              Default font family
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="58822032">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/58822032/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you are using Android Studio 3.5+, Changing font is super simple. Select the text widget on Design view and check fontFamily on Attribute Window. The value dropdown contains all the available fonts from which you can select one. If you are looking for Google Fonts, Click More Fonts option.
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Attribute Window
             </strong>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7E1xn.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Attribute Window" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/7E1xn.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             <strong>
              Google Fonts
             </strong>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xzUjM.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="Google Fonts" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/xzUjM.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="post-layout--right js-post-comments-component">
           <div class="comments js-comments-container bt bc-black-075 mt12" data-min-length="15" data-post-id="58822032" id="comments-58822032">
            <ul class="comments-list js-comments-list" data-addlink-disabled="true" data-canpost="false" data-cansee="true" data-comments-unavailable="false" data-remaining-comments-count="0">
             <li class="comment js-comment" data-comment-id="113351034" data-comment-owner-id="1544044" data-comment-score="0" id="comment-113351034">

         <div class="post-layout">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/22934035/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             With some trial and error I learned the following.
            </p>
            <p>
             Within the *.xml you can combine the stock fonts with the following functions, not only with typeface:
            </p>
            <pre><code> android:fontFamily="serif" 
 android:textStyle="italic"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             With this two styles, there was no need to use typeface in any other case. The range of combinations is much more bigger with fontfamily&amp;textStyle.
            </p>
           </div>

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can also do this by adding a font folder under the res directory like below.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/F4Dj3.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/F4Dj3.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Then, selecting Font as the resource type.
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nEEb5.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/nEEb5.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             You can find avaliable fonts from
             <a href="https://www.1001fonts.com/" rel="noreferrer">
              https://www.1001fonts.com/
             </a>
             , and then extracting the TTF files to this font directory.
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/qHX6l.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/qHX6l.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Finally, just change the XML file that contains your textview by adding android:fontFamily:"@font/urfontfilename"
            </p>
            <p>
             <a href="https://i.stack.imgur.com/FI9WW.png" rel="noreferrer">
              <img alt="enter image description here" src="https://i.stack.imgur.com/FI9WW.png"/>
             </a>
            </p>
           </div>

        <a name="28849594">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="28849594" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="20" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="5" id="answer-28849594" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="28849594">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="5" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             5
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/28849594/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             The valid value of android:fontFamily is defined in /system/etc/system_fonts.xml(4.x) or /system/etc/fonts.xml(5.x). But Device Manufacturer might modify it, so the actual font used by setting fontFamily value depends on the above-mentioned file of the specified device.
            </p>
            <p>
             In AOSP, the Arial font is valid but must be defined using "arial" not "Arial", for example
             <strong>
              android:fontFamily="arial"
             </strong>
             . Have a qucik look at Kitkat's system_fonts.xml
            </p>
            <pre><code>    &lt;family&gt;
    &lt;nameset&gt;
        &lt;name&gt;sans-serif&lt;/name&gt;
        &lt;name&gt;arial&lt;/name&gt;
        &lt;name&gt;helvetica&lt;/name&gt;
        &lt;name&gt;tahoma&lt;/name&gt;
        &lt;name&gt;verdana&lt;/name&gt;
    &lt;/nameset&gt;
    &lt;fileset&gt;
        &lt;file&gt;Roboto-Regular.ttf&lt;/file&gt;
        &lt;file&gt;Roboto-Bold.ttf&lt;/file&gt;
        &lt;file&gt;Roboto-Italic.ttf&lt;/file&gt;
        &lt;file&gt;Roboto-BoldItalic.ttf&lt;/file&gt;
    &lt;/fileset&gt;
&lt;/family&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             //////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////
            </p>
            <p>
             There are three relevant xml-attributes for defining a "font" in layout--
             <strong>
              android:fontFamily
             </strong>
             ,
             <strong>
              android:typeface
             </strong>
             and
             <strong>
              android:textStyle
             </strong>
             . The combination of "fontFamily" and "textStyle" or "typeface" and "textStyle" can be used to change the appearance of font in text, so does used alone. Code snippet in
             <strong>
              TextView.java
             </strong>
             like this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>    private void setTypefaceFromAttrs(String familyName, int typefaceIndex, int styleIndex) {
    Typeface tf = null;
    if (familyName != null) {
        tf = Typeface.create(familyName, styleIndex);
        if (tf != null) {
            setTypeface(tf);
            return;
        }
    }
    switch (typefaceIndex) {
        case SANS:
            tf = Typeface.SANS_SERIF;
            break;

        case SERIF:
            tf = Typeface.SERIF;
            break;

        case MONOSPACE:
            tf = Typeface.MONOSPACE;
            break;
    }
    setTypeface(tf, styleIndex);
}


    public void setTypeface(Typeface tf, int style) {
    if (style &gt; 0) {
        if (tf == null) {
            tf = Typeface.defaultFromStyle(style);
        } else {
            tf = Typeface.create(tf, style);
        }

        setTypeface(tf);
        // now compute what (if any) algorithmic styling is needed
        int typefaceStyle = tf != null ? tf.getStyle() : 0;
        int need = style &amp; ~typefaceStyle;
        mTextPaint.setFakeBoldText((need &amp; Typeface.BOLD) != 0);
        mTextPaint.setTextSkewX((need &amp; Typeface.ITALIC) != 0 ? -0.25f : 0);
    } else {
        mTextPaint.setFakeBoldText(false);
        mTextPaint.setTextSkewX(0);
        setTypeface(tf);
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             From the code We can see:
            </p>
            <ol>
             <li>
              if "fontFamily" is set, then the "typeface" will be ignored.
             </li>
             <li>
              "typeface" has standard and limited valid values. In fact, the values are "normal" "sans" "serif" and "monospace", they can be found in system_fonts.xml(4.x) or fonts.xml(5.x). Actually both "normal" and "sans" are the default font of system.
             </li>
             <li>
              "fontFamily" can be used to set all fonts of build-in fonts, while "typeface"  only provide the typical fonts of "sans-serif" "serif" and "monospace"(the three main category of font type in the world).
             </li>
             <li>
              When only set "textStyle", We actually set the default font and the specified style. The effective value are "normal" "bold" "italic" and "bold | italic".
             </li>
            </ol>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             Here is an
             <strong>
              easier wa
             </strong>
             y that can work in some cases. The principle is to add a not visible TextVview in your xml layout and to
             <strong>
              get its typeFace
             </strong>
             in the java code.
            </p>
            <p>
             The layout in the xml file:
            </p>
            <pre><code> &lt;TextView
        android:text="The classic bread is made of flour hot and salty. The classic bread is made of flour hot and salty. The classic bread is made of flour hot and salty."
        android:layout_width="0dp"
        android:layout_height="0dp"
        android:fontFamily="sans-serif-thin"
        android:id="@+id/textViewDescription"/&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And the java code:
            </p>
            <pre><code>myText.setTypeface(textViewSelectedDescription.getTypeface());
</code></pre>
            <p>
             It has worked for me (within a TextSwitcher for example).
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             Try this:
            </p>
            <pre><code>TextView textview = (TextView) findViewById(R.id.textview);

Typeface tf= Typeface.createFromAsset(getAssets(),"fonts/Tahoma.ttf");
textview .setTypeface(tf);
</code></pre>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="62424804" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="23" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="4" id="answer-62424804" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="62424804">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="4" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             4
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/62424804/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             To set the font by program, write...
            </p>
            <pre><code>     TextView tv7 = new TextView(this);
     tv7.setText(" TIME ");    
     tv7.setTypeface(Typeface.create("sans-serif-condensed",Typeface.BOLD));
     tv7.setTextSize(12);
     tbrow.addView(tv7);
</code></pre>
            <p>
             The name "sans-serif-condensed" is referenced from fonts.xml file which should be created in app--&gt; res--&gt; values folder and it holds the fonts in it.
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;resources&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_light"&gt;sans-serif-light&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_medium"&gt;sans-serif-medium&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_regular"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_condensed"&gt;sans-serif-condensed&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_black"&gt;sans-serif-black&lt;/string&gt;
    &lt;string name="font_family_thin"&gt;sans-serif-thin&lt;/string&gt;
&lt;/resources&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Hope this is clear!
            </p>
           </div>
