        <a name="43885389">
        </a>
        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="43885389" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="25" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="3" id="answer-43885389" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="43885389">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="3" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             3
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/43885389/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             If you want to use a TextView in so many places with same font family, extend the TextView class and set your font like this:-
            </p>
            <pre><code>public class ProximaNovaTextView extends TextView {

    public ProximaNovaTextView(Context context) {
        super(context);

        applyCustomFont(context);
    }

    public ProximaNovaTextView(Context context, AttributeSet attrs) {
        super(context, attrs);

        applyCustomFont(context);
    }

    public ProximaNovaTextView(Context context, AttributeSet attrs, int defStyle) {
       super(context, attrs, defStyle);

       applyCustomFont(context);
    } 

    private void applyCustomFont(Context context) {
        Typeface customFont = FontCache.getTypeface("proximanova_regular.otf", context);
        setTypeface(customFont);
    }
}
</code></pre>
            <p>
             And then use this custom class in xml for the TextView like this:-
            </p>
            <pre><code>   &lt;com.myapp.customview.ProximaNovaTextView
        android:id="@+id/feed_list_item_name_tv"
        android:layout_width="match_parent"
        android:layout_height="wrap_content"
        android:textSize="14sp"
        /&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="44326259" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="26" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="2" id="answer-44326259" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="44326259">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

              </path>
             </svg>

            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/44326259/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             I just want to mention that the hell with the fonts inside Android is about to end, because this year on Google IO we finally got this -&gt;
             <a href="https://developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html" rel="nofollow noreferrer">
              https://developer.android.com/preview/features/working-with-fonts.html
             </a>
            </p>
            <p>
             Now there is a new resource type a
             <strong>
              font
             </strong>
             and you can place all your application fonts inside res/fonts folder and access then with R.font.my_custom_font, just like you can access
             <strong>
              string
             </strong>
             res values,
             <strong>
              drawable
             </strong>
             res values etc. You have even chance to create
             <strong>
              font-face
             </strong>
             xml file, which is gonna be set of your custom fonts (about italic, bold and underline attr).
            </p>
            <p>
             Read the link above for more info. Let's see the support.
            </p>
           </div>

            <p>
             The new font resource allows to directly set
             <code>
              font
             </code>
             using
            </p>
            <pre><code>android:fontFamily="@font/my_font_in_font_folder"
</code></pre>

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="63784735">

               </path>

            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/63784735/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">

              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You can define a custom FontFamily like this:
            </p>
            <p>
             <code>
              /res/font/usual.xml
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?&gt;
&lt;font-family xmlns:tools="http://schemas.android.com/tools"
    xmlns:android="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res/android"
    xmlns:app="http://schemas.android.com/apk/res-auto"
    tools:ignore="UnusedAttribute"&gt;
    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="normal"
        android:fontWeight="200"
        android:font="@font/usual_regular"
        app:fontStyle="normal"
        app:fontWeight="200"
        app:font="@font/usual_regular" /&gt;

    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="italic"
        android:fontWeight="200"
        android:font="@font/usual_regular_italic"
        app:fontStyle="italic"
        app:fontWeight="200"
        app:font="@font/usual_regular_italic" /&gt;

    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="normal"
        android:fontWeight="600"
        android:font="@font/usual_bold"
        app:fontStyle="normal"
        app:fontWeight="600"
        app:font="@font/usual_bold" /&gt;

    &lt;font
        android:fontStyle="italic"
        android:fontWeight="600"
        android:font="@font/usual_bold_italic"
        app:fontStyle="italic"
        app:fontWeight="600"
        app:font="@font/usual_bold_italic" /&gt;
&lt;/font-family&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Now you can do
            </p>
            <pre><code>android:fontFamily="@font/usual"
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Assuming your other
             <code>
              font
             </code>
             resources are there as well, with lowercase letters and
             <code>
              _
             </code>
             s.
            </p>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">

         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="28476869">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">

             </svg>

              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">

            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/28476869/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">

          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             You set style in
             <code>
              res/layout/value/style.xml
             </code>
             like that:
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;style name="boldText"&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:textStyle"&gt;bold|italic&lt;/item&gt;
    &lt;item name="android:textColor"&gt;#FFFFFF&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             and to use this style in
             <code>
              main.xml
             </code>
             file use:
            </p>
            <pre><code>style="@style/boldText"
</code></pre>
           </div>

        <div class="answer js-answer" data-answerid="53138856" data-highest-scored="0" data-parentid="12128331" data-position-on-page="30" data-question-has-accepted-highest-score="1" data-score="1" id="answer-53138856" itemprop="suggestedAnswer" itemscope="" itemtype="https://schema.org/Answer">
         <div class="post-layout">
          <div class="votecell post-layout--left">
           <div class="js-voting-container d-flex jc-center fd-column ai-stretch gs4 fc-black-200" data-post-id="53138856">
            <button aria-label="Up vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-up-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowUpLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 25h32L18 9 2 25Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div class="js-vote-count flex--item d-flex fd-column ai-center fc-black-500 fs-title" data-value="1" itemprop="upvoteCount">
             1
            </div>
            <button aria-label="Down vote" aria-pressed="false" class="js-vote-down-btn flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-selected-classes="fc-theme-primary" data-unselected-classes="" title="This answer is not useful">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconArrowDownLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
              <path d="M2 11h32L18 27 2 11Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </button>
            <div aria-label="Accepted" class="js-accepted-answer-indicator flex--item fc-green-500 py6 mtn8 d-none" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" role="note" tabindex="0" title="Loading when this answer was accepted…">
             <div class="ta-center">
              <svg aria-hidden="true" class="svg-icon iconCheckmarkLg" height="36" viewbox="0 0 36 36" width="36">
               <path d="m6 14 8 8L30 6v8L14 30l-8-8v-8Z">
               </path>
              </svg>
             </div>
            </div>
            <a aria-label="Timeline" class="js-post-issue flex--item s-btn s-btn__unset c-pointer py6 mx-auto" data-controller="s-tooltip" data-ks-title="timeline" data-s-tooltip-placement="right" data-shortcut="T" href="/posts/53138856/timeline" title="Show activity on this post.">
             <svg aria-hidden="true" class="mln2 mr0 svg-icon iconHistory" height="18" viewbox="0 0 19 18" width="19">
              <path d="M3 9a8 8 0 1 1 3.73 6.77L8.2 14.3A6 6 0 1 0 5 9l3.01-.01-4 4-4-4h3L3 9Zm7-4h1.01L11 9.36l3.22 2.1-.6.93L10 10V5Z">
              </path>
             </svg>
            </a>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="answercell post-layout--right">
           <div class="s-prose js-post-body" itemprop="text">
            <p>
             For android-studio 3 and above you can use this style and then all
             <code>
              textView
             </code>
             font change in app.
            </p>
            <p>
             create this style in your
             <code>
              style.xml
             </code>
             :
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;!--OverRide all textView font--&gt;
&lt;style name="defaultTextViewStyle" parent="android:Widget.TextView"&gt;
        &lt;item name="android:fontFamily"&gt;@font/your_custom_font&lt;/item&gt;
&lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
            <p>
             Then use it in your theme :
            </p>
            <pre><code>&lt;!-- Base application theme. --&gt;
    &lt;style name="AppTheme" parent="Theme.AppCompat.Light.NoActionBar"&gt;
        &lt;!-- Customize your theme here. --&gt;
        &lt;item name="colorPrimary"&gt;@color/colorPrimary&lt;/item&gt;
        &lt;item name="colorPrimaryDark"&gt;@color/colorPrimaryDark&lt;/item&gt;
        &lt;item name="colorAccent"&gt;@color/colorAccent&lt;/item&gt;
        &lt;item name="android:textViewStyle"&gt;@style/defaultTextViewStyle&lt;/item&gt;
    &lt;/style&gt;
</code></pre>
           </div>
           <div class="mt24">
            <div class="d-flex fw-wrap ai-start jc-end gs8 gsy">
